Otherwise, returns cmputil.DiffReport\n   544→func (alertRule *AlertRule) Diff(rule *AlertRule, ignore ...string) cmputil.DiffReport {\n   545→\tvar reporter cmputil.DiffReporter\n   546→\tops := make([]cmp.Option, 0, 6)\n   547→\n   548→\t// json.RawMessage is a slice of bytes and therefore cmp's default behavior is to compare it by byte, which is not really useful\n   549→\tvar jsonCmp = cmp.Transformer(\"\", func(in json.RawMessage) string {\n   550→\t\tb, err := json.Marshal(in)\n   551→\t\tif err != nil {\n   552→\t\t\treturn string(in)\n   553→\t\t}\n   554→\t\treturn string(b)\n 560→\t\tjsonCmp,\n   561→\t\tcmpopts.EquateEmpty(),\n   562→\t)\n   563→\n   564→\tif len(ignore) > 0 {\n   565→\t\tops = append(ops, cmpopts.IgnoreFields(AlertRule{}, ignore...))\n   566→\t}\n   567→\tcmp.Equal(alertRule, rule, ops...)\n   568→\treturn reporter.Diffs\n   569→}\n   570→\n   571→// SetDashboardAndPanelFromAnnotations will set the DashboardUID and PanelID field by doing a lookup \"The Grafana unified alerting (ngalert) subsystem is a comprehensive alert rule evaluation, state management, and notification system. Here's a detailed map of the major components and their interactions:\\n\\n## Architecture Overview\\n\\nThe unified alerting system is organized into five primary components located in `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/services/ngalert/`:\\n\\n### 1. Alert Rule Storage (Models Layer)\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/models/`\\n\\nThe models layer defines the core data structures for the alerting system:\\n- **AlertRule** (`alert_rule.go`): The central alert rule entity with properties like UID, title, condition, query data, notification settings, and evaluation schedule (interval, for duration)\\n- **AlertRuleGroup** (`alert_rule.go`): Groups alert rules by folder and interval\\n- **AlertInstance** (`instance.go`): Represents individual alert instances with state, labels, and timing information\\n- **InstanceStateType** (`constants.go`): Enumeration of alert states (Alerting, Normal, Pending, NoData, Error, Recovering)\\n- **NoDataState and ExecutionErrorState** (`constants.go`): Configuration enums for handling missing data and execution failures\\n\\nThese models are persisted and retrieved via the RulesStore interface for scheduling operations.\\n\\n### 2. Scheduler Component\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/`\\n\\nThe scheduler orchestrates periodic evaluation of alert rules:\\n- **ScheduleService** interface (`schedule.go`): Main entry point with `Run(context.Context) error` method\\n- **schedule** struct (internal): The core scheduler manages:\\n  - Rule registry (`registry.go`) tracking active rules and their state\\n  - Rule fetcher (`fetcher.go`) that retrieves alert rules from the database via RulesStore interface\\n  - Evaluation sequence (`sequence.go`) ensuring rules are evaluated in order per organization/group\\n  - Retry logic (`retry.go`) for failed evaluations\\n  - Jitter strategy (`jitter.go`) to distribute evaluation load\\n  - Ticker (`schedule/ticker/ticker.go`) for time-based scheduling\\n\\n**Key Interfaces:**\\n- **RulesStore**: Fetches alert rules via `GetAlertRulesForScheduling()`\\n- **AlertsSender**: Routes evaluated alerts to the notifier\\n- **RecordingWriter**: Persists recording rule results to datasources\\n- **AlertRuleStopReasonProvider**: Determines stop reason for rules\\n\\n**Data Flow:** The scheduler's `Run()` method continuously fetches rules, evaluates them using the eval package, processes results through the state manager, and sends notifications.\\n\\n### 3. State Manager Component\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/state/`\\n\\nThe state manager maintains alert instance state and handles state transitions:\\n- **State** struct (`state.go`): Represents current state of an alert instance including:\\n  - Current state (Normal, Alerting, NoData, Error, Recovering)\\n  - FiredAt, ResolvedAt, LastSentAt timestamps\\n  - Evaluation results and error information\\n  - Image snapshot of the alert\\n  - Annotations and labels\\n\\n- **Manager** struct (`manager.go`): Central orchestrator that:\\n  - Maintains in-memory cache of alert states (`cache.go`)\\n  - Persists state changes via StatePersister interface\\n  - Records state transitions in history via Historian interface\\n  - Manages image capture for alert visualization\\n  - Handles state retention policies\\n\\n- **StateTransition** struct (`state.go`): Encapsulates state changes between evaluation cycles\\n\\n**Key Interfaces:**\\n- **AlertInstanceManager**: Query interface for current alert states\\n- **StatePersister**: Handles async and sync state persistence with multiple implementations:\\n  - `persister_async.go`: Asynchronous batch persistence\\n  - `persister_sync.go`: Synchronous per-rule persistence\\n  - `persister_sync_rule.go`: Per-rule synchronous variant\\n  - `persister_noop.go`: No-op implementation for testing\\n- **InstanceStore**: Saves/loads alert instances from database\\n- **ImageCapturer**: Captures screenshots for alert visualization\\n- **Historian**: Records state transitions for audit trail\\n\\n**State Transitions:** The manager orchestrates transitions between states, ensuring proper timing for alert firing (pending → alerting) and resolution. It maintains resend delays to re-notify after resolution.\\n\\n### 4. History Writer (State Historian)\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/`\\n\\nThe historian provides audit trail and historical state querying:\\n- **Historian** interface: `WriteStateTransition(ctx, transition, instanceKey)` records state changes\\n- **Backend** interface (`backend.go`): Abstract backend with multiple implementations:\\n  - **AnnotationBackend** (`annotation.go`): Stores history as dashboard annotations\\n  - **RemoteLokiBackend** (`loki.go`): Sends to Grafana Loki for log-based storage\\n  - **RemotePrometheusBackend** (`prometheus.go`): Sends to Prometheus remote write endpoint\\n  - **MultipleBackend** (`multiple.go`): Chains multiple backends for redundancy\\n  - **NoopBackend** (`noop.go`): No-op implementation\\n\\n- **Querier** interface (`query.go`): Retrieves historical state data\\n- **RuleMeta** struct (`model/rule.go`): Metadata for rules in historical records\\n\\n**Data Flow:** When state transitions occur in the Manager, the Historian receives `WriteStateTransition()` calls which are forwarded to configured backends. This provides a complete audit trail of alert state changes.\\n\\n### 5. Notifier Component (Alertmanager Integration)\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/`\\n\\nThe notifier integrates with Prometheus Alertmanager for alert grouping, routing, and notifications:\\n- **Alertmanager** interface (`alertmanager.go`): Main notifier with operations:\\n  - `ApplyConfig()`: Apply notification routing configuration\\n  - `PutAlerts()`: Receive evaluated alerts\\n  - `GetAlerts()`: Query current alerts\\n  - `CreateSilence()` / `DeleteSilence()`: Silence management\\n  - `GetReceivers()`: List notification receivers\\n  - `GetStatus()`: Query alertmanager status\\n\\n- **MultiOrgAlertmanager** (`multiorg_alertmanager.go`): Manages separate Alertmanager instances per organization\\n\\n- **AlertingSender** (`sender.go`): Sends PostableAlerts to Alertmanager\\n- **ReceiverService** (`receiver_svc.go`): Manages notification receiver configurations\\n- **SilenceService** (`silence_svc.go`): Manages alert silences\\n\\n**Key Interfaces:**\\n- **AlertingStore**: Persistence layer for notification configuration\\n- **Crypto**: Encrypts/decrypts sensitive notification settings\\n\\n**Legacy Support:** `legacy_storage/` provides backward compatibility with older alerting configurations.\\n\\n**Configuration:** `alertmanager_config.go` handles Alertmanager configuration including routes, receivers, grouping, and notification templates.\\n\\n## Component Interactions\\n\\n1. **Scheduler → Rules Storage**: ScheduleService.Run() → RulesStore.GetAlertRulesForScheduling()\\n2. **Scheduler → Evaluator**: schedule.evaluateRule() → Evaluator.Evaluate() (from eval package)\\n3. **Evaluator → State Manager**: Alert evaluation results flow to Manager.ApplyResult()\\n4. **State Manager → State Persistence**: Manager.ApplyResult() → StatePersister.Sync() → InstanceStore.SaveAlertInstance()\\n5. **State Manager → Historian**: StateTransitions → Historian.WriteStateTransition() → Backend implementations\\n6. **Historian → Storage Backends**: RuleMeta and state changes sent to Annotation, Loki, or Prometheus backends\\n7. **State Manager → Alertmanager**: Manager sends alert state changes to AlertsSender → Alertmanager.PutAlerts()\\n8. **Alertmanager → Notification**: Alertmanager routes alerts through Receivers to external notification systems\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Interface-driven architecture**: Heavy use of interfaces (ScheduleService, AlertsSender, RulesStore, etc.) enables testing and pluggable implementations\\n- **Multi-backend pattern**: Historian supports multiple backends (Annotation, Loki, Prometheus, None) for flexibility\\n- **State machine**: Alert instances transition through defined states with proper validation\\n- **Async persistence**: Batch and async state saving reduces database load\\n- **Per-organization isolation**: Separate Alertmanager instances per organization ensure data isolation\\n\\nThe unified alerting system is production-ready with comprehensive state management, historical tracking, and flexible notification routing.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4688,"cache_read_input_tokens":32546,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4688},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a6fd228a-073c-450f-b626-e708d3cd5478","uuid":"feb95ce9-44fc-4a9e-9f8c-e1304f431dd3"}

\"The Grafana unified alerting (ngalert) subsystem is a comprehensive alert rule evaluation, state management, and notification system. Here's a detailed map of the major components and their interactions:\\n\\n## Architecture Overview\\n\\nThe unified alerting system is organized into five primary components located in `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/services/ngalert/`:\\n\\n### 1. Alert Rule Storage (Models Layer)\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/models/`\\n\\nThe models layer defines the core data structures for the alerting system:\\n- **AlertRule** (`alert_rule.go`): The central alert rule entity with properties like UID, title, condition, query data, notification settings, and evaluation schedule (interval, for duration)\\n- **AlertRuleGroup** (`alert_rule.go`): Groups alert rules by folder and interval\\n- **AlertInstance** (`instance.go`): Represents individual alert instances with state, labels, and timing information\\n- **InstanceStateType** (`constants.go`): Enumeration of alert states (Alerting, Normal, Pending, NoData, Error, Recovering)\\n- **NoDataState and ExecutionErrorState** (`constants.go`): Configuration enums for handling missing data and execution failures\\n\\nThese models are persisted and retrieved via the RulesStore interface for scheduling operations.\\n\\n### 2. Scheduler Component\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/`\\n\\nThe scheduler orchestrates periodic evaluation of alert rules:\\n- **ScheduleService** interface (`schedule.go`): Main entry point with `Run(context.Context) error` method\\n- **schedule** struct (internal): The core scheduler manages:\\n  - Rule registry (`registry.go`) tracking active rules and their state\\n  - Rule fetcher (`fetcher.go`) that retrieves alert rules from the database via RulesStore interface\\n  - Evaluation sequence (`sequence.go`) ensuring rules are evaluated in order per organization/group\\n  - Retry logic (`retry.go`) for failed evaluations\\n  - Jitter strategy (`jitter.go`) to distribute evaluation load\\n  - Ticker (`schedule/ticker/ticker.go`) for time-based scheduling\\n\\n**Key Interfaces:**\\n- **RulesStore**: Fetches alert rules via `GetAlertRulesForScheduling()`\\n- **AlertsSender**: Routes evaluated alerts to the notifier\\n- **RecordingWriter**: Persists recording rule results to datasources\\n- **AlertRuleStopReasonProvider**: Determines stop reason for rules\\n\\n**Data Flow:** The scheduler's `Run()` method continuously fetches rules, evaluates them using the eval package, processes results through the state manager, and sends notifications.\\n\\n### 3. State Manager Component\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/state/`\\n\\nThe state manager maintains alert instance state and handles state transitions:\\n- **State** struct (`state.go`): Represents current state of an alert instance including:\\n  - Current state (Normal, Alerting, NoData, Error, Recovering)\\n  - FiredAt, ResolvedAt, LastSentAt timestamps\\n  - Evaluation results and error information\\n  - Image snapshot of the alert\\n  - Annotations and labels\\n\\n- **Manager** struct (`manager.go`): Central orchestrator that:\\n  - Maintains in-memory cache of alert states (`cache.go`)\\n  - Persists state changes via StatePersister interface\\n  - Records state transitions in history via Historian interface\\n  - Manages image capture for alert visualization\\n  - Handles state retention policies\\n\\n- **StateTransition** struct (`state.go`): Encapsulates state changes between evaluation cycles\\n\\n**Key Interfaces:**\\n- **AlertInstanceManager**: Query interface for current alert states\\n- **StatePersister**: Handles async and sync state persistence with multiple implementations:\\n  - `persister_async.go`: Asynchronous batch persistence\\n  - `persister_sync.go`: Synchronous per-rule persistence\\n  - `persister_sync_rule.go`: Per-rule synchronous variant\\n  - `persister_noop.go`: No-op implementation for testing\\n- **InstanceStore**: Saves/loads alert instances from database\\n- **ImageCapturer**: Captures screenshots for alert visualization\\n- **Historian**: Records state transitions for audit trail\\n\\n**State Transitions:** The manager orchestrates transitions between states, ensuring proper timing for alert firing (pending → alerting) and resolution. It maintains resend delays to re-notify after resolution.\\n\\n### 4. History Writer (State Historian)\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/`\\n\\nThe historian provides audit trail and historical state querying:\\n- **Historian** interface: `WriteStateTransition(ctx, transition, instanceKey)` records state changes\\n- **Backend** interface (`backend.go`): Abstract backend with multiple implementations:\\n  - **AnnotationBackend** (`annotation.go`): Stores history as dashboard annotations\\n  - **RemoteLokiBackend** (`loki.go`): Sends to Grafana Loki for log-based storage\\n  - **RemotePrometheusBackend** (`prometheus.go`): Sends to Prometheus remote write endpoint\\n  - **MultipleBackend** (`multiple.go`): Chains multiple backends for redundancy\\n  - **NoopBackend** (`noop.go`): No-op implementation\\n\\n- **Querier** interface (`query.go`): Retrieves historical state data\\n- **RuleMeta** struct (`model/rule.go`): Metadata for rules in historical records\\n\\n**Data Flow:** When state transitions occur in the Manager, the Historian receives `WriteStateTransition()` calls which are forwarded to configured backends. This provides a complete audit trail of alert state changes.\\n\\n### 5. Notifier Component (Alertmanager Integration)\\n\\n**Location:** `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/`\\n\\nThe notifier integrates with Prometheus Alertmanager for alert grouping, routing, and notifications:\\n- **Alertmanager** interface (`alertmanager.go`): Main notifier with operations:\\n  - `ApplyConfig()`: Apply notification routing configuration\\n  - `PutAlerts()`: Receive evaluated alerts\\n  - `GetAlerts()`: Query current alerts\\n  - `CreateSilence()` / `DeleteSilence()`: Silence management\\n  - `GetReceivers()`: List notification receivers\\n  - `GetStatus()`: Query alertmanager status\\n\\n- **MultiOrgAlertmanager** (`multiorg_alertmanager.go`): Manages separate Alertmanager instances per organization\\n\\n- **AlertingSender** (`sender.go`): Sends PostableAlerts to Alertmanager\\n- **ReceiverService** (`receiver_svc.go`): Manages notification receiver configurations\\n- **SilenceService** (`silence_svc.go`): Manages alert silences\\n\\n**Key Interfaces:**\\n- **AlertingStore**: Persistence layer for notification configuration\\n- **Crypto**: Encrypts/decrypts sensitive notification settings\\n\\n**Legacy Support:** `legacy_storage/` provides backward compatibility with older alerting configurations.\\n\\n**Configuration:** `alertmanager_config.go` handles Alertmanager configuration including routes, receivers, grouping, and notification templates.\\n\\n## Component Interactions\\n\\n1. **Scheduler → Rules Storage**: ScheduleService.Run() → RulesStore.GetAlertRulesForScheduling()\\n2. **Scheduler → Evaluator**: schedule.evaluateRule() → Evaluator.Evaluate() (from eval package)\\n3. **Evaluator → State Manager**: Alert evaluation results flow to Manager.ApplyResult()\\n4. **State Manager → State Persistence**: Manager.ApplyResult() → StatePersister.Sync() → InstanceStore.SaveAlertInstance()\\n5. **State Manager → Historian**: StateTransitions → Historian.WriteStateTransition() → Backend implementations\\n6. **Historian → Storage Backends**: RuleMeta and state changes sent to Annotation, Loki, or Prometheus backends\\n7. **State Manager → Alertmanager**: Manager sends alert state changes to AlertsSender → Alertmanager.PutAlerts()\\n8. **Alertmanager → Notification**: Alertmanager routes alerts through Receivers to external notification systems\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Interface-driven architecture**: Heavy use of interfaces (ScheduleService, AlertsSender, RulesStore, etc.) enables testing and pluggable implementations\\n- **Multi-backend pattern**: Historian supports multiple backends (Annotation, Loki, Prometheus, None) for flexibility\\n- **State machine**: Alert instances transition through defined states with proper validation\\n- **Async persistence**: Batch and async state saving reduces database load\\n- **Per-organization isolation**: Separate Alertmanager instances per organization ensure data isolation\\n\\nThe unified alerting system is production-ready with comprehensive state management, historical tracking, and flexible notification routing.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
